TAPE - Training for Audiovisual Preservation in Europe 
The carriers for audiovisual documents are fragile and 
subject to rapid decay: the lifespan of most tapes, even 
when stored under good  conditions, is measured in 
decades. Continued access is further complicated because 
evolving technolog y forces equipment out of use. 
Digitization of audiovisual materials would enhance the 
chances of their survival and facilitate access, but is as yet 
expensive and little applied outside the large institutions. 
TAPE, funded under the Culture 2000 programme  of the 
EU, was a project for raising awareness and training by 
expert meetings, research, publications and workshops. 
TAPE focused on audiovisual collec tions held outside the 
major national institutions with specific responsibilities for 
audiovisual heritage. 
EU-
Culture 
2000 
2008 http://www.tape-
online.net/ 
DELOS - Network of Excellence on Digital Libraries. 
The DELOS network is conducting a joint progra m of 
activities aimed at integrating and coordinating the 
ongoing research activities of the major Euro pean teams 
working in Digital Library - related areas with the goal of 
developing the next generation Digital Library 
technologies. DELOS intends to conduct a joint programme 
of activities aimed at coordinating current European 
research in DL -related areas, with the goal of developing 
the next generation of DL technologies. 
The Phonogrammarchiv brought in its expertise to bear on 
work within the Preservation Cluster.

Brief description of the organization:  
CulturArts is a public entity integrated in the Conselleria d’Educació, Cultura i Esport whose aim is the 
development and execution of the cultural policies of the Generalitat Valenciana as for concerns to the 
knowledge, protection, promotion, preservation, restoration, estudy, research and dissemination of the 
scenic, musical and plastic arts in all their varieties an d the museums in particular, and of the audiovisual 
heritage and cinematography and, in general, of all the cultural goods of the valencian cultural heritage.  
To achieve a higher administrative coordination and a closer work relationship between the diffe rent 
cultural areas, CulturArts consists of and assume the responsibilities in subjects of Music, Audio visual and 
Cinematography (IVAC), Theatre and Dance, Preservation and Restoration of Cultural Goods (IVC+R) and 
Castelló Cultural, which inform the sub-directorates of CulturArts.  
CulturArts-IVAC is the sub -directorate that developes the responsibilities for the audiovisual and 
cinematographical subjects and in particular all regarded to the safeguarding of the audiovisual heritage, 
including its recopilation, preservation, restoration, cataloguing and dissemination.

PARTNER 15 - DFI 
Full name: Deutsches Filminstitut  
Frankfurt am Main 
Web page: www.deutsches-filminstitut.de 
Country: Spain  
Type: RO 
 
Brief description of the organization:  
The Deutsches Filminstitut – DIF e.V. was founded in 1949 and is the oldest and one of the most important  
institutions in the Federal Republic for the collection, archiving and academic utilisation of films a nd film-
historical documentation, as well as for the transmission of film culture and film literacy. It is a recognised 
non-profit institution and is supported by both public funds and private benefactors. Since 2006 it has been 
the organising institute fo r the formerly municipal Deutsches Filmmuseum, with its exhibition and cinema 
facilities and activities.  
 
The film archive department of DIF preserves a  collection of more than 20.000 films, which are stored 
according to modern conservation standards in c limate controlled vaults. The collection is comprised of 
feature films, fiction and documentaries, as well as short films among these promotional and inf ormational 
films as well as amateur footage. 
 
DIF is a full member of the Fédération Internationale des  Archives du Film (FIAF), the Association des 
Cinémathèques Européenes (ACE) and the Deutscher Kinemateksverbund (Association of German 
Cinématheques). 
Aside from its functions as research institute, museum and archive, DIF is actively engaged in promoting  
film culture in the scope of several national and international online projects. With filmportal.de, DIF runs 
the national filmography providing users w ith information, photos, texts, etc. on German film and 
filmmakers from the beginnings to the present. On European level, since 2006, DIF has been co-ordinating a 
series of EU -funded projects, such as MIDAS, which built the online union catalogue for Europ ean film 
archives filmarchives-online.eu (2006-2009), EFG - The European Film Gateway, a portal for dig ital content 
from European filmarchives (2009 -2011) and EFG1914, a film digitisation project on World War I (2012 -
2014).  
Role in the Project:  
Definition of packaging specifications and validation process.

PARTNER 16 - ALINARI 
Full name : Fratelli Alinari Istituto d Edizioni 
Artistiche SpA 
Web page: www.alinari.com 
Country: Italy 
Type: SME 
 
Brief description of the organization:  
Founded in Florence in 1852, Fratelli Alinari is the oldest firm in the world working in the field o f 
photography, the image and communication.  The birth of photography and the story of the Firm go hand in 
hand in their development and growth, as attested to by the immense Alinari owned fund of 5.000.000 
photographs. 
This fund is continuously growing and, thanks to a rational policy of new acquisitions and new photographic 
campaigns, it ranges from daguerreotypes to modern color photos. 
In 1852 Leopoldo Alinari, with his brothers Giuseppe and Romualdo, founded the photographic workshop, 
heart of the firm that still bears his name. It was the beginning of a unique endeavor that specialized in 
photographic portraiture, views of works of art and historical monuments, and achieved immediate national 
and international renown. 
Today the name of Alinari guarantees a century of experience and state of the art professional technology. 
In 2001 the Digital Archive was inaugurated. It continues to grow and progress constantly with images that 
can be consulted on line.  
Alinari is a leader in Photographic Publishing, and its Art Printworks or Art Printworks is the only one in the 
NEMOSINE part B H2020 NMBP-35-2017 
 
Page 95 of 109 
 
world still using the artisan technique of collotype on paper and on silver plate from photographic images.  
The Alinari laboratory engages in conservation treatment of the many types  of materials that comprise the 
photographic heritage: from the oldest daguerreotypes to calotypes, to various types of photographic prints, 
rare negativ es on paper and Conservation and restoration also includes covering the other aspects of the 
photographic heritage comprised of frames, albums, particularly valuable and fragile containers in leather, 
wood, mother of pearl, semi -precious stones, bronze. The restoration laboratory has also activated a section 
specialized in digital restoration, working with electronic supports in constructing images that are illegible as 
a result of damage due to atmospheric or mechanical agents.  These new methodologies make  it possible to 
virtually reconstruct images that would otherwise be irretrievably lost, where the leve l of deterioration 
excludes the possibility of a traditional type of restoration. This greatly increases the chances for the 
recovery of visual documents and the entire wealth of information they carry. 
collodion and silver glass-plate negatives, up to the most recent color proofs and negatives.

The involvement of IRIS (Innovació i Recerca Industrial i Sostenible, S.L., SME) as a Linked Th ird Party of 
VISUM will allow to increase the level of excellence of the technica l work planned in the project  both in 
terms of industrial integration. VISUM is 100% owned by IRIS which is its founder. 
IRIS is an advanced engineering company that specialis es in process monitoring and contro l, and process 
optimisation. Its commercial division offers advanced monitoring and control solutions based on NIR and  
hyperspectral imaging solutions for foreign body detection and chemical composition analysis; data 
management solutions for data processi ng, decision support, automation and data analysis (big production 
data).  
Besides, IRIS’ innovation division has 4 core lines: 
1. Optical and spectroscopy technologies (e.g. MEMs spectrophotometers, fluorescence and Rama n) 
for process monitoring for on-line and PAT applications in food, pharmaceuticals and the process industries 
2. SMAC technologies: information technologies and data management 
3. Novel processing technologies (ultrasound, plasma, microwave…) for process intensification and 
non-thermal decontamination   
4. Sustainable processing technologies: waste valorisation strategies, biocompounds and biopackaging 
for the circular economy 
The company was established in 2007 and currently employs 56 staff with a turnov er of €3.8 M. It is 
equipped with engineering workshops (3), food testing and wet chemistry laboratory, optics labs (2), and an 
electronics/telecommunications lab. IRIS is ISO 9001:2008 certified and also is certified under UNE -EN-ISO 
166002: Management Systems R&D&i.  
With its team includi ng telecom and electronics engineers, system engineering, application programming 
and web development etc. IRIS can carry out full system des ign and engineering, including electronic design 
(PCB) and assembly, firmware an d software development, electrical harnesses and interconnections. 
Moreover IRIS has mechanical and mechatronics engineers, specialised in process upscaling, integration 
work, as well as installation, validation and industrialisation of prototypes and equi pment in different 
industries. In a ddition to this broad cross -disciplinary engineering team, IRIS’ research team consisting 
among other of food and material scientists, biolog ists and physicists, have all the expertise to validate the 
technologies develop ed. Finally, IRIS has significant e xpertise in the use of QFD (quality function 
deployement) and uses a systems development management approach based on KANBAN agile 
methodologies

Task 3.1. Development of nanofibre based carriers with incorporated MOFs and antifungals  
One part of this task will address the scalability and manufacturing of the novel delivery platforms incorporating 
MOFs and antifungals to address challenges associated with production of large -scale carriers. In particular, this 
will involve technologically impr oved equipment, using enha nced powerful electrodes and by varying the 
geometries and shapes of the counter electrodes. Man ufacturing reproducibility of nanofibrous carriers in 
particular with regard to their internal structure will also be validated in thi s task. The scaled-up engineered and 
validated carrier prototypes will be prepared for serial production. Standardisation,  reproducibility and scale-up 
protocols will also be developed and verified in an operational environment. For this purpose, we have to lease 
the operating line using Nanospider technology. 
Total costs: Operating line renting: costs 10.000 € (renting 8 days/8 hours - special Nanospider technology)

NOA GmbH NOA GmbH will act as subcontractor in work packages 1, 6 and 8. 
NOA is the leading global pro vider of flexible turnkey solutions for quality -controlled digitizing, management, 
and archiving of audio and other media content. Scalable to suit collections of al l sizes, NOA's product families, 
ingestLINE™, mediARC™, act LINE ™ and jobDB™, not only help  ensure long-term preservation of media, 
but also support enterprise -wide collaboration, efficiency, a nd productivity by enabling fast and accurate 
identification and retrieval of clips from the full range of an enterprise's arch ive. NOA's easy-to-use proprietary 
technologies are today installed in some 20 high -profile enterprises worldwide, including Sver iges Radio 
Förvaltnings (SRF), Yleisradio Finland (YLE), Radiotelevizija  Slovenija (RTV), Fonoteca Nacional de Mexico, 
the Vlaamse Radio- en Televisieomroep (VRT), and Voice of Vietnam. With headquarters in Vienna, Austria, 
NOA is committed to the ongoing development of innovative technologies to ensure the maintenance of 
invaluable cultural heritage for future generations. 
NOA will contribute its existing considerable chemical  and mechanical testing laboratory facilities, as well as 
extended special cond ition storage and testing facilities. Additionally, NO A will contribute as consu lting 
company in the sales strategy of such an application into the market.  
Specifically, NOA will participate in  WP1: defintion of the requirements of CH artefacts  and supporting in the 
preparation and analysis of Deliver able 1 .1. Previous data for initial development of models, by providing 
chemical and mechani cal testing laboratory facilities, laboratory assistant to run the tests (e.g. SPME/GC -MS), 
WP6: Materials evaluation: validation of package  design and efficacy (acidity t esting, accelerated ageing, 
functionality, applicabil ity, audiovisual s ignal quality evaluation). WP 8: Contribution to business mode l, 
communication and dissemination ( Marketing and management / Business Model Development, ma rketing 
strategy, networking wi thin audiovisual communities & heritage institutions as well as their u mbrella 
organisations, e.g. IASA, FIAT).

5. ETHICS AND SECURITY
5.1 ETHICS 
The project does not face ethical issues except for the possible ones raised in relat ion w ith the human beings 
involvement, but any of those data are not sensitive ones. These issues will be linked to the correct fulfilment of 
the inf ormation consent forms and proper use of the information sheets due to the  participation of humans 
beings a nd th e related procedures and criteria to identify/recruit research participants that will be followed 
within the NEMOSINE project (i.e. participatio n of  humans beings for the interviews on the prototypes 
performance, under WP6 and WP8).  
 
The selection process for participants, using data bases must comply with the European and national legislations.  
All partners involved in the mentioned WPs will pa rticipate in the work with human beings (for collection of data, 
interviews). 
 
This could reflect privacy -sensitive occupancy information that may emerge when multiple sources of data are 
combined. Such personal information will be stored in an encrypted form and the identifiers will be in a password 
protected file, therefore no  personal information will be ava ilable to the general public outside few members of 
the NEMOSINE team. Specifically, the partners will take all necessary steps to ensure that the In formation is "de-
identified", i.e. that all Personal Data is removed from the provided information, made il legible, or otherwise 
made inaccessible to the receiving parties prior to provision (in accordance with Article 2 section (a) of the 
European Data Protection Directive). 
 
Each party shall be responsible for ensuring its own  compliance with all laws and reg ulations applicable to its 
activities, including without limitation the acquisition of data, the processing of data by it through any tool used in 
connection with the Project and the use of such data within the project framework. Such laws include, but are not 
limited to, those in respect of rights of privacy, publicity, reputation and intellectual property rights, including 
patent and copyright rights. 
 
We will make sure that we keep with H2020 guidelines in terms of recrui tment, informed consent, data sto rage, 
protection and destruction procedures (no personal information will be collected during surveys, which will be 
anonymous, not involve minors nor any audio or video recording).

• 'EU-classified information' as background or results: NO

Innovative packaging solutions for storage and conservation of 20th century cultural 
heritage of artefacts based on cellulose derivate  
(NMBP35-2017: Innovative solutions for the conservation of 20th century cultural 
heritage)  
 
I, the undersigned Elena Badea, identified with national identity document series PA, 
number 094447, as President of the Asociatia Stiinta si patrimoniul cultural in 
conexiune1 (i-CON) based in Bulevardul Tineretului no. 51 , bloc 64, sc.1, apt 34, 
Bucharest, postal code  040352, Romania, hereby declare  that Asociatia Stiinta si 
patrimoniul cultural in conexiune is interested in the results that will be obtained from 
the project “Innovative packaging solutions for storage and conservation of 20th 
century cultural heritage of artefacts based on cellulose derivate ”, to be submitted to 
the NMBP35-2017 call:  Innovative solutions for the conservation of 20th century 
cultural heritage. 
In my capacity as President  consider that the outcomes of the “Innovative packaging 
solutions for storage and conservation of 20th century cultural heritage of artefacts 
based on cellulose der ivate” according to the proposed workplan could be very 
interesting as alternative to the solutions currently used. Therefore, i-CON Association 
wishes to support the Project and hereby commits to follow the Project developments.
